Subdomain: Speciality

<action>

</action>

<action>
TYPE [17940] [X123456789]
</action>
 - TYPE target_role=textbox target_label=E-mail used on order * value=buckeye.foobar@gmail.com example=TYPE [22288] [buckeye.foobar@gmail.com]
<action>
TYPE [22288] [buckeye.foobar@gmail.com]
</action>
 - CLICK target_role=button target_label=View value= example=CLICK [26636]
<action>
